Instead of using F3, try using MSI Afterburner because the F3 menu actually takes up power from your client's performance. This usually isn't the case for higher end computers, plus OBS or any other recording software can put some HEAVY lag on your game. I recommend using external devices or putting it on a LAN server with a separate client instead of ReplayMod so the testing client doesn't get put on more pressure from mods. Funny how nobody notices that at 1:05 you see the debug screen of the "100$ computer" but on the right side of the screen you can clearly see that the cpu in use is a Intel core i7-9750H, which is a laptop cpu (NOT A DESKTOP CPU), and most of the laptops (for example dell or lenovo ones) that come with this cpu have a dedicated gpu like an 1650, a 1660/1660Ti, or more expensive ones a 2060, but he literally uses the integrated graphics, which obviously performance wise does not even compare with one of the above mentioned dedicated gpus. Also he didn't mention anything of optimizing the devices, such as removing bloat, cleaning up the installation, disabling useless services, replacing thermal paste, or maybe TO USE A CAPTURE CARD ON AN EXTERNAL PC and not obs studio which takes a significant amount of resources for low end devices which in other words means it reduces FPS.
